A planned long term project for the discontinued use of a high volume wave solder machine which utilized lead based solder has been largely achieved.  The lead based wave solder machine was decomissioned on June 15, 2013 and, although the plant is not 100% lead-free, the change in raw materials affects the majority of products being manufactured at this plant.  This change has enabled the site to "graduate" from the EPCRA Section 313 Toxic Release Inventory (TRI) program as the site no longer triggers the 100 pound reporting threshold for lead.
